    17‚Üídef read_file_with_retry(filepath, max_attempts=5):

    20‚Üí            # Wait for file to stabilize before reading

    33‚Üídef wait_for_file_complete(filepath, timeout=10): # Reduced timeout for faster testing
    34‚Üí    start_time = time.time()
